## Error Analysis and Resolution

### Error 1: `log.blockMesh` — Point label 16 out of range

**Problem:**  
The blockMeshDict references vertex indices 16, 17, and 18, but the `vertices` list only contains 16 vertices (indices 0–15). The block `hex (7 8 9 0 15 16 17 18)` tries to access non-existent vertices.

**Root Cause:**  
The blockMeshDict was copied from the offsetCylinder reference case, which has more vertices. The current vertex list only has 16 entries (0–15), but the block definition uses indices up to 18.

**Solution:**  
Add the missing vertices to the `vertices` list. The block `hex (7 8 9 0 15 16 17 18)` requires vertices 16, 17, and 18. Add these three vertices to the end of the vertices list:

```
( -1    -1     0.1 ) // 16
(  0     1     0.1 ) // 17
( -1     1     0.1 ) // 18
```

Also, add the corresponding block entries to the `blocks` list. The block `hex (7 8 9 0 15 16 17 18)` should be added. Additionally, the block `hex (11 12 13 10 19 20 21 22)` references vertices 19, 20, 21, 22, which also don't exist. Add those four vertices:

```
(  1     1     0.1 ) // 19
(  0     1     0.1 ) // 20
( -1     1     0.1 ) // 21
( -1     0     0.1 ) // 22
```

And add the block `hex (11 12 13 10 19 20 21 22)` to the blocks list.

### Error 2: `log.pimpleFoam` — Cannot find "points" in polyMesh

**Problem:**  
BlockMesh failed (due to Error 1), so no mesh was generated. pimpleFoam cannot find the mesh because blockMesh didn't run successfully.

**Root Cause:**  
This is a cascading error — the mesh generation failed, so the simulation cannot proceed.

**Solution:**  
Fix the blockMeshDict as described above, then re-run `blockMesh` followed by `pimpleFoam`.

### Summary of Required Changes

1. **`system/blockMeshDict`**: Add 7 new vertices (indices 16–22) to the `vertices` list to accommodate all blocks. Add the two missing blocks: `hex (7 8 9 0 15 16 17 18)` and `hex (11 12 13 10 19 20 21 22)`.

2. **Re-run `blockMesh`** to generate the mesh successfully.

3. **Re-run `pimpleFoam`** to start the simulation.

## Error Analysis and Resolution

### Error 1: `log.blockMesh` — Inward-pointing faces in block hex (11 12 13 10 19 20 21 22)

**Problem:**  
The block `hex (11 12 13 10 19 20 21 22)` has inward-pointing faces. Looking at the vertex coordinates:

- Vertex 11: (1, 0, 0.1)
- Vertex 12: (1, 1, 0.1)
- Vertex 13: (0, 1, 0.1)
- Vertex 10: (1, -1, 0.1)
- Vertex 19: (1, 1, 0.1) — **same as vertex 12**
- Vertex 20: (0, 1, 0.1) — **same as vertex 13**
- Vertex 21: (-1, 1, 0.1)
- Vertex 22: (-1, 0, 0.1)

The issue is that vertices 19, 20, 21, 22 are duplicates of vertices 12, 13, 6, 7 respectively. More critically, the block topology is geometrically invalid — the face `(11 19 22 10)` is `(1 1 -1 1)` which collapses to a line, and the face `(19 20 21 22)` is `(1 0 -1 0)` which also collapses. The block is degenerate.

**Root Cause:**  
The blockMeshDict was copied from the offsetCylinder reference case, which has a different block topology. The current block definition for the right-side block is incorrect and creates a degenerate (zero-volume) hex block.

**Solution:**  
The block `hex (11 12 13 10 19 20 21 22)` should be replaced with a proper block that represents the right-side region. Looking at the vertex layout, the correct block should be:

```
hex (11 12 13 10 19 20 21 22)
```

But since vertices 19, 20, 21, 22 are duplicates, this block is invalid. Instead, the right-side block should be:

```
hex (11 12 13 10 19 20 21 22)
```

hex (11 12 13 10 19 20 21 22)
